# Results by syntax

For readablility some shortcuts are applied:

- `named`
  - `named: 'named'`
- `[named]`
  - `[named]: 'named'` (non enumerable)
- `default`
  - `default: 'default'`
- `[default]`
  - `[default]: 'default'` (non enumerable)
- `__esModule`
  - `__esModule: true`
- `[__esModule]`
  - `[__esModule]: true` (non enumerable)
- `[G]`
  - `[Getter]`
- `[Module]`

  - `[Symbol(Symbol.toStringTag)]: 'Module'`

- ðŸ’Ž hard outlier
- ðŸŸ¡ outlier
- âœ… very common value

<!-- syntax results -->
